Question #438 (ID: 78349)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Why is education important for people?

Options:
a. It helps in personal and professional development.
b. It is not important.
c. It only benefits the rich.
d. It is a waste of time.


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the core function of education — it provides knowledge, skills, and critical thinking that help individuals grow personally and perform better in jobs and society.  
Step 2: Reasoning — with education people gain qualifications, improve problem-solving and communication abilities, and access better opportunities, so it directly promotes both personal and professional development.  
Conclusion: therefore option (a) is correct. Options (b), (c), and (d) are incorrect because they contradict observable effects of education: it is important, benefits people across economic backgrounds, and is not a waste of time.

Explanation:

Question #439 (ID: 78350)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What did you learn from 'The Parrot's Tale' about education?

Options:
a. Education is essential for growth.
b. Education is overrated.
c. Education is only for children.
d. Education has no impact.


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Recall the story’s central message — the parrot gains knowledge, understanding, and confidence through learning, which helps it grow and improve its life.  
Step 2: Compare this message with each option: option (a) matches directly because the story shows education enabling growth; options (b), (c), and (d) contradict the story’s events and theme.  
Step 3: Conclude that the correct answer is (a) Education is essential for growth, because the parrot’s progress in the tale demonstrates the positive, transformative impact of education.

Question #440 (ID: 77710)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What does the proverb 'Give a person a fish and you feed them for a day; teach a person to fish and you feed them for a lifetime' mean?

Options:
a. Education is only about memorizing facts.
b. Teaching skills is more beneficial than just providing resources.
c. It is better to work alone than to help others.
d. Money is more important than knowledge.


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Interpret the proverb — giving a fish represents short-term help (one meal), while teaching to fish represents giving a lasting skill that provides long-term self-sufficiency.  
Step 2: Compare this meaning with the choices and select the one that matches: option b states that teaching skills is more beneficial than just providing resources, which matches the proverb.  
Step 3: Why the others are incorrect — option a is wrong because the proverb emphasizes skills and independence, not rote memorization; option c is wrong because the proverb encourages empowering others, not isolation; option d is wrong because it values knowledge/skill over mere money.  
Therefore the correct answer is b.

Explanation:

Question #449 (ID: 76492)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In the context of education, how can we compare traditional learning with modern technology-based learning?

Options:
a. Traditional learning is always better.
b. Technology-based learning lacks personal touch.
c. Both have their unique advantages and disadvantages.
d. Modern learning is only for urban students.


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Read each option and test it against the general evidence about learning methods.  
Step 2: Evaluate options:
- Option a claims an absolute superiority of traditional learning — this is too strong because traditional methods have strengths (face-to-face interaction, social skills) but also limitations (fixed pace, limited resources).  
- Option b points out a real issue: some technology-based learning can feel less personal, but many tech tools (video calls, adaptive platforms) can be highly interactive and personalized.  
- Option d wrongly generalizes that modern learning is only for urban students; in fact, technology can reach rural areas (e.g., mobile learning, offline resources) though access may vary.  
Conclusion: Option c is correct because it acknowledges that both traditional and technology-based learning have unique advantages and disadvantages, so a balanced comparison best reflects reality.

Question #452 (ID: 76092)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Analyze the consequences of the bird’s education in the story. What do you think would have happened if the bird had received proper care and learning instead of just training?

Options:
a. The bird would have become a great singer.
b. The bird would have died earlier.
c. The bird would have thrived and communicated effectively.
d. The bird would have confused the trainers.


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
সমাধান:
1) ধাপ ১: সমস্যাটির মূল বিশ্লেষণ — গল্পে পাখিটিকে কেবল যান্ত্রিকভাবে প্রশিক্ষণ করা হয়েছে, মানসিক তত্ত্ব, যত্ন ও বাস্তব শিক্ষা মেলেনি; ফলত তার স্বাস্থ্য, আচরণ ও যোগাযোগ দুর্বল ছিল।  
2) ধাপ ২: বিকল্প পরিস্থিতি—যদি পাখিটিকে যথাযথ যত্ন ও শিক্ষা দেওয়া হত, তাহলে তার মানসিক বিকাশ, সামাজিক দক্ষতা ও ভাষাগত প্রতিক্রিয়া উন্নত হতো এবং সে শান্তিপূর্ণভাবে পরিবেশের সঙ্গে খাপ খাইয়ে নিয়ে কার্যকরভাবে যোগাযোগ করতে পারত।  
3) ধাপ ৩: বিকল্পগুলোর তুলনা — বিকল্প c ("The bird would have thrived and communicated effectively") সরাসরি উপরের অনুমানের সঙ্গে মিলে; a খুব নির্দিষ্ট ও অনিশ্চিত (সকল শিক্ষিত পাখি ‘দারুণ গায়ক’ হবে না), b বিপরীত এবং অযৌক্তিক, এবং d অপ্রাসঙ্গিক কারণ ভাল শিক্ষা সাধারণত বিভ্রান্তি বাড়ায় না।  
সঠিক উত্তর: c

Question:
What is the main idea of the proverb, "Give a person a fish and you feed them for a day; teach a person to fish and you feed him for a lifetime?"

Options:

b. Fishing is the best way to survive.
c. People should only receive food.
d. Education is not necessary.


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution: The proverb contrasts short-term aid with long-term empowerment — giving a fish feeds someone for a day, while teaching them to fish enables lifelong self-sufficiency. Therefore the central idea is that teaching (or enabling skills) is more important than merely providing immediate help, so option a is correct. Options b, c, and d are incorrect because (b) takes the metaphor literally, (c) contradicts the proverb’s emphasis on learning rather than only receiving, and (d) states the opposite of the proverb’s message.

Question #460 (ID: 73736)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In 'The Parrot’s Tale,' what was the primary purpose of educating the bird?

Options:
a. To teach it to sing beautifully
b. To ensure it stops eating fruits
c. To enhance its overall value as a creature
d. To provide it with a lavish cage


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the bird’s stated purpose for education in the story — the narrator explains that the bird was taught manners, speech, and useful behaviours to make it more valuable and respectable.  
Step 2: Match that purpose to the options: “to enhance its overall value as a creature” directly corresponds to improving its worth through education.  
Therefore the correct answer is (c).

Explanation of other options: (a) teaching it to sing beautifully is a limited, specific skill and not the main goal; (b) stopping it from eating fruits is not an educational aim in the text; (d) providing a lavish cage is about environment, not about educating the bird.

Explanation:

Question:
What consequence did excessive focus on form over substance have on the bird's education?

Options:
a. The bird learned to recite scriptures
b. The bird became healthier
c. The bird eventually died
d. The bird learned to interact better with others


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Read the stem — excessive focus on form over substance means attention was given to outward appearances or rituals while essential needs or real learning were neglected.  
Step 2: From that premise the logical consequence is that the bird’s true well‑being and proper care were ignored, so it suffered fatal consequences; hence the correct answer is (c) the bird eventually died.  
Step 3: Options (a) and (d) imply positive educational outcomes which contradict “substance” being neglected, and (b) (became healthier) is the opposite of the expected result when essential needs are ignored.

Question:
What role do EdTech companies play in education?

Options:
a. They replace teachers.
b. They provide funding for schools.
c. They develop AI tools for classrooms.
d. They monitor student behavior.


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Solution:
1. Read the option meanings and identify the typical activities of EdTech companies: they design and deliver technology for learning (platforms, apps, analytics, and increasingly AI-driven tools).
2. Compare each option to that role:
   - a is incorrect: EdTech generally augments teachers’ work rather than fully replacing them.
   - b is incorrect: providing funding is not the main role of EdTech companies (that’s more a role for governments, donors, or investors).
   - c is correct: many EdTech companies develop AI tools for classrooms (adaptive learning, automated grading, personalized tutoring).
   - d is misleading: while some tools include analytics that can track engagement, “monitor student behavior” is neither their primary nor sole role.
3. Therefore the best choice is c.

Question:
What is one advantage of AI in education?

Options:
a. It can completely replace teachers.
b. It provides personalized learning experiences.
c. It requires no human interaction.
d. It is inexpensive to implement.


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Read the options and identify which describes a realistic advantage of AI in education.  
Step 2: Evaluate each option:
- Option a is incorrect because AI can assist teachers but cannot fully replace the variety of human roles (motivation, emotional support, classroom management).  
- Option c is incorrect because AI systems usually require human interaction for guidance, oversight, and contextual judgment.  
- Option d is incorrect because implementing AI often involves significant costs for software, hardware, and training.  
Step 3: Option b is correct because AI can analyze a learner’s performance and adapt content, pace, and feedback to individual needs, thereby providing personalized learning experiences.

Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

Step 3: Eliminate incorrect options — (a) is wrong because volunteerism is not always planned; (b) is wrong because civic engagement can also be organized; (c) is wrong because volunteerism may be part of academic programs but that is not its defining difference.

Question #484 (ID: 24119)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কিভাবে 'The Parrot's Tale' এবং 'Education and Technology' গল্প দুটি শিক্ষার গুরুত্ব এবং প্রযুক্তির ভূমিকা তুলে ধরে?

Options:
a. শিক্ষা শুধুমাত্র পরীক্ষার ফলাফল অর্জনের জন্য জরুরি, প্রযুক্তির কোনো প্রয়োজন নেই।
b. শিক্ষা এবং প্রযুক্তি উভয়ই শিক্ষার্থীদের অভিজ্ঞতাকে সমৃদ্ধ করতে পারে, তবে প্রযুক্তির ব্যবহার সঠিকভাবে করতে হবে।
c. প্রযুক্তি শিক্ষার বিকল্প হতে পারে যা শিক্ষককে অপ্রয়োজনীয় করে দেয়।
d. শিক্ষার উদ্দেশ্য শুধুমাত্র চাকরি পাওয়া, প্রযুক্তি এর সাথে সম্পর্কিত নয়।


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সমাধান:
1. ধাপে ধাপে চিন্তা: গল্প দুটিই শিক্ষার গুরুত্বকে উচ্চ মূল্য দেয় — একদিকে জ্ঞান, নৈতিকতা ও শেখার অনুষঙ্গ (The Parrot's Tale) এবং অন্যদিকে আধুনিক সময়ে শিক্ষা প্রক্রিয়াকে প্রযুক্তি সাহায্য করে কিভাবে (Education and Technology) তা তুলে ধরা হয়।  
2. তুলনামূলক বিশ্লেষণ: দুটোই দেখায় যে প্রযুক্তি নিজে লক্ষ্য নয় বরং শিক্ষাকে সমৃদ্ধ ও সহজতর করার একটি উপায়; সঠিক ব্যবহার থাকলে তা শিক্ষার্থীর অভিজ্ঞতা ও শেখার গুণমান বাড়ায়।  
3. সিদ্ধান্ত: তাই b সঠিক কারণ এটি বলে শিক্ষা ও প্রযুক্তি উভয়ই গুরুত্বপূর্ণ কিন্তু প্রযুক্তির খাপ খাওয়ানো ও সঠিক ব্যবহার অপরিহার্য।  
4. অন্য বিকল্পগুলোর সংক্ষিপ্ত ব্যাখ্যা: a ও d অতিরিক্ত সংকীর্ণ — গল্পগুলো শিক্ষাকে কেবল পরীক্ষা বা চাকরির মাত্রা পর্যন্ত সীমাবদ্ধ করে না; c ভুল কারণ গল্পগুলো প্রযুক্তিকে শিক্ষককে বদলে দেয়নি বরং শিক্ষককে সহায়কারী হিসেবে দেখায়।

Explanation:

Question #485 (ID: 8046)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What is the main theme of 'The Parrot's Tale' by Rabindranath Tagore?

Options:
a. The importance of external appearances
b. The futility of education without understanding
c. The necessity of leisure in education
d. The benefits of teamwork in learning


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Recall the story — the parrot can recite lessons and scriptures perfectly but has no understanding or freedom; his life is mechanical recitation without inner comprehension.  
Step 2: Identify the theme — Tagore criticizes mere rote learning and shows that education or knowledge without true understanding and inner freedom is useless.  
Step 3: Eliminate other options — external appearances (a) is not the focus; leisure in education (c) and teamwork (d) are not themes in this tale.  

Answer: option (b) The futility of education without understanding.

Explanation:

Question #486 (ID: 8047)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What type of educational work does 'The Parrot’s Tale' represent?

Options:
a. Tragedy
b. Satire
c. Comedy
d. Biography


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Determine the work’s tone and purpose — "The Parrot’s Tale" uses humor, irony and allegorical episodes to expose human follies and criticize social or moral problems.  
Step 2: Match those features to a genre — such use of ridicule and indirect moral criticism is characteristic of satire.  
Therefore the correct answer is (b) Satire.  
Briefly why others are incorrect: tragedy focuses on serious suffering and downfall, comedy aims primarily for laughter without sustained moral criticism, and biography is a factual life account; none fit the allegorical, critical nature of "The Parrot’s Tale."

Explanation:

Question #487 (ID: 8048)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What is the main theme reflected in 'The Parrot's Tale' regarding education?

Options:
a. Education should focus solely on academic knowledge.
b. Education's true value is in teaching practical skills for life.
c. Education is only for the wealthy.
d. Education is about acquiring wealth and status.


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the central message of "The Parrot's Tale" — the story emphasizes how learning useful, everyday skills and wisdom helps the parrot survive and thrive.  
Step 2: Compare that message to the options: a narrows education to academics only, which contradicts the tale; c and d claim education is about wealth or exclusive privilege, which the story does not promote.  
Step 3: Conclude that option b best matches the theme because the tale highlights education’s practical value in real life rather than purely academic, wealthy, or status-based aims.

Therefore the correct answer is: b.

Question #488 (ID: 8049)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What was a significant outcome of the King's visit to see the educational progress of the bird in 'The Parrot's Tale'?

Options:
a. The bird sang beautifully.
b. The King realized the bird was neglected despite the efforts.
c. The bird learned to fly again.
d. The bird became the favorite of the court.


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Recall the scene in the story where the King inspects the bird’s education and observes its condition and progress.  
Step 2: The King notices that despite lessons and effort, the bird shows signs of neglect and lack of proper care; therefore he realizes the bird was neglected despite the efforts — this corresponds to option (b).  
Step 3: Options (a), (c), and (d) are incorrect because the story does not emphasize the bird singing beautifully, regaining flight, or becoming the court’s favorite as the King’s principal conclusion; the key outcome is the King’s realization of neglect.

Question #489 (ID: 6814)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In 'The Parrot's Tale', what was the primary reason the King ordered the education of the bird?

Options:
a. The bird was a threat to the kingdom.
b. The bird was not singing properly.
c. The bird was seen as useless and needed improvement.
d. The bird was a royal pet.


Correct Answer: c

Solution:
সমাধান: কাহিনীর প্রেক্ষাপে প্রধান তথ্যটি খুঁজে নিলে বোঝা যায় যে রাজা পাখিটিকে শিক্ষিত করার নির্দেশ দিয়েছিলেন কারণ পাখিটিকে অকার্যকর বা নিষ্প্রয়োজনীয় হিসেবে দেখা হচ্ছিল এবং তাকে উন্নত করা চাইছিল — তাই সঠিক উত্তর (c) "The bird was seen as useless and needed improvement." অন্যান্য বিকল্পগুলি ভুল কারণ (a) কাহিনীতে পাখিটি রাজ্যের জন্য কোনো সরাসরি হুমকি ছিল না, (b) কেবল গান না গাওয়ার কোনো উল্লেখ ছিল না যে সেটিই প্রধান কারণ, এবং (d) যদিও পাখিটি রাজপরিবারের কাছে পরিচিত হতে পারে, কিন্তু শিক্ষার আদেশ দেওয়ার মূল কারণ সেটি রাজপ্রাসাদের পোষা জন্তু হওয়া নয়।

Question #490 (ID: 6811)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What is the ultimate goal of education as per the proverb mentioned in 'The Parrot's Tale'?

Options:
a. To gain wealth
b. To teach a person to fish
c. To pass exams
d. To memorize scriptures


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: The proverb in "The Parrot's Tale" emphasizes making a person self-reliant—giving skills so they can support themselves (analogous to teaching someone to fish rather than handing them fish).  
Step 2: Option b ("To teach a person to fish") directly matches this idea of education aiming for independence and practical ability.  
Step 3: The other options are narrower or instrumental: gaining wealth, passing exams, or memorizing scriptures are possible outcomes but not the ultimate, broad goal implied by the proverb.  
Therefore the correct answer is: b.

Explanation:

In 'The Parrot's Tale', what did the King realize was neglected in the education of the bird?

Options:
a. The quality of the cage
b. The bird's basic needs
c. The amount of knowledge provided
d. The teachers' qualifications


Correct Answer: b

Solution:
Solution: Read the story details and identify what the King observed about the bird's upbringing. He noticed the bird had learned facts but was deprived of care, comfort and basic needs (food, affection, proper care), so the neglected area was the bird's basic needs — option b. Options a, c and d are incorrect because the story did not focus on the cage quality, the sheer amount of knowledge, or the teachers' qualifications.

Question #492 (ID: 6813)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: English For Today | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What does the proverb 'Give a person a fish and you feed them for a day; teach a person to fish and you feed him for a lifetime' emphasize about education?

Options:
a. Education is not important.
b. Education has short-term benefits.
c. Education should provide long-lasting skills.
d. Education is only for the wealthy.


Correct Answer: c

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Interpret the proverb — giving a fish meets an immediate need (short-term help), while teaching to fish gives a person the skill to provide for themselves repeatedly (long-term benefit).

Step 2: Match this interpretation to the options. The proverb emphasizes lasting ability and self-sufficiency, which corresponds to option (c): education should provide long-lasting skills.

Step 3: Eliminate other options: (a) is wrong because the proverb values a form of help (teaching), not dismissing education; (b) is wrong because it contrasts short-term aid with long-term training, so the emphasis is on long-term, not short-term benefits; (d) is wrong because the proverb applies universally, not only to the wealthy.

Therefore the correct answer is (c).

Explanation:
